//「どうだろうねぇ＠梨花ちゃんってあれでなかなかうまいから！＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 3, "ps3/s19/03/990300355", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「どうだろうねぇ。",
		   NULL, "\"Eu me pergunto.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 3, "ps3/s19/03/990300356", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "梨花ちゃんってあれでなかなかうまいから！」",
		   NULL, " A Rika-chan é muito boa nessas coisas!\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//「あぁ、それは同感＠　頭を撫でる罰ゲーム、あれきっと梨花ちゃんだぜ。＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#956f6e>圭一</color>", NULL, "<color=#956f6e>Keiichi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 1, "ps3/s19/01/hr_kei08490", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「あぁ、それは同感！",
		   NULL, "\"Sim, sinto a mesma coisa!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 1, "ps3/s19/01/hr_kei08500", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　頭を撫でる罰ゲーム、あれきっと梨花ちゃんだぜ。」",
		   NULL, " Essa penalidade de acariciar cabeças provavelmente foi escrito pela Rika-chan.\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(2, 3, "sprite/me1a_def_a1_", "0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 200, TRUE );

//「私も同感～＠　校長先生の頭を撫でられるのは梨花ちゃんだけだし。￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>魅音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Mion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 3, "ps3/s19/03/990300357", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「私も同感〜！",
		   NULL, "\"Também achei isso~!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 3, "ps3/s19/03/990300358", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　校長先生の頭を撫でられるのは梨花ちゃんだけだし。」",
		   NULL, " Afinal, a única que poderia se safar dando tapinhas na cabeça dele é a Rika-chan.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();


//　とりとめのないおしゃべり＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　とりとめのないおしゃべり。",
		   NULL, "Apenas jogando conversa fora.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//　夕方の空気とひぐらしの声が、熱かった今日一日の熱をやさしく冷ましてくれた￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　夕方の空気とひぐらしの声が、熱かった今日一日の熱をやさしく冷ましてくれた。",
		   NULL, "O dia quente parecia estar sendo resfriado pelo canto das cigarras.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
